My strong points have been to travel and learn about cultures all over the world. I have applied them to my life experiences in Real Estate, Interior Design, Floral Designs and Architectural Photography. This has led to a serenity and confidence in my abilities to contribute this knowledge to family and community. My goal now is to create POETIC visions through photography after three decades of travel (BEFORE DIGITAL) and studying displays in Museums worldwide. I will be adding macro photography in the coming weeks to my website. This will give an even closer look at nature in a specialized venue. See website: artisticphotovisions.vpweb.com for a look at my photos over a 30 year period without digital technology.</p></div></div><div class=""treasury-container no-server-fetch facelift""><div Visions</a></h5></header><span class=""experience-date-locale""><time>August 1997</time>  Present (19 years 2 months)<span class=""locality"">Online</span></span><p class=""description summary-field-show-more"" dir=""ltr"">ALL OF MY PHOTOS AROUND THE WORLD WERE TAKEN WITH MANY DIFFERENT CAMERAS BEFORE DIGITAL. My worldwide photo art is to promote interest in our everyday surroundings, to appreciate geological formations and to provide a VERY close-up look at the world. Traveling worldwide sparked my interest in world history and especially art history. This led to an intellectual pursuit to study many subjects and cultures. This has led to an appreciation which I am trying to share through a newly created website. It is still a work in progress - as am I. ""artisticphotovisions.vpweb.com."" Macro Photography is a new challenge in learning about precise presentations. Taking a workshop from a Master of Macro, Mike Moats, will hopefully lead to the images I want to create. I think Georgia O'Keefe would be amazed at our advanced technology. I hope to set an example that women are architects of change through the different stages of life.</p><dl class=""education-associated""><dt data-trk-code=""prof-exp-snippet-endorsement-close"" data-trk-code-alt=""prof-exp-snippet-endorsement-open""><span>(Open)</span>2 recommendations</dt><dd class=""associated-endorsements ""><ul><li class=""row-first""><a href=""https://www.linkedin.com/profile/view?id=AAEAAAqfBRoBXMmaJP4TrU57bExd5EN1lb843CU&amp;authType=name&amp;authToken=P98Z&amp;trk=prof-exp-snippet-endorsement-photo"" class=""associated-photo""><img width=""38"" height=""38"" class=""lazy-load"" src=""https://static.licdn.com/scds/common/u/img/spacer.gif"" data-li-src=""https://media.licdn.com/mpr/mpr/shrink_100_100/p/1/000/27c/272/1ba2a0e.jpg"" alt=""Andrea Bittle""/></a><hgroup><h5><span data-tracking=""endorser"" class=""new-miniprofile-container /profile/mini-profile-with-connections?_ed=0_29tCtIvlLd-4270DiGb-8h"" data-li-url=""/profile/mini-profile-with-connections?_ed=0_29tCtIvlLd-4270DiGb-8h"" data-li-tl=""tl/shared/profile/mini_profile_shell""><strong><a href=""https://www.linkedin.com/profile/view?id=AAEAAAqfBRoBXMmaJP4TrU57bExd5EN1lb843CU&amp;authType=name&amp;authToken=P98Z&amp;trk=prof-exp-snippet-endorsement-name"">Andrea Bittle</a></strong></span></h5><h6>Teacher. A conference of any kind in Budapest showed a high level of multi-cultural competency. World R. E.
